With Stagelight, you can make beats, mix loops or even create full multi-track songs with drum, instrument, audio and vocal tracks.  \r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\nStagelight includes the following features at no cost: \r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\nLessons and tutorials including:  \r\n\r\n- Building a beat \r\n\r\n- Learning how to record instruments \r\n\r\n- Editing audio and MIDI \r\n\r\n- Mixing \r\n\r\n- much more! \r\n\r\n \r\n\r\nLoopBuilder:  Make music like a DJ! \r\n\r\nLoopBuilder is a loop-style production feature that enables anyone to build music quickly by adding, arranging and triggering audio, drum, instrument or vocal loops either individually or in groups, complete with automatic beat syncing. It doesn‚Äôt matter if you‚Äôre just starting out, a seasoned DJ or a professional music producer, LoopBuilder is a fun, easy and powerful tool for making all styles of music. \r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n 9 Built-in instruments including: \r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\nDrum Machine: \r\n\r\n- Over 50 Drum kit and Pattern Presets included \r\n\r\n- Integrated step sequencer \r\n\r\n- AutoFill: swipe to create simple beats with a single gesture \r\n\r\n- Advanced Automation   \r\n\r\n- Build your own kits with sample importing \r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n \r\n\r\nSampleVerse: a hybrid sampler and synthesizer instrument. Key Lock allows you to maintain the proper key and scale of your song without ever hitting a bad note. \r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\nAudio recording:  \r\n\r\nRecord audio using your device‚Äôs built-in microphone or any ASIO or Class Compliant audio device. \r\n\r\n  \r\n\r\nMIDI device support: \r\n\r\nStagelight supports your favorite MIDI devices with true plug and play support.
